2.4.4 Formål med lenke (3 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Link has no accessible name (empty link) (×75 across article pages)

Add text content, aria-label, or image with alt text
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Link opens in new window without indication (×37 across article pages)

Add text like '(opens in new tab)' or use visually-hidden text for screen readers
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MINOR

Link text has redundant phrase: 'Gå til toppen' (×15 across article pages)

<a class="css-irbjyk" href="/#top" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_self"><div class="css-in0oqx"><div><div class="css-a501gl">Gå til toppen</div></div><span><div class="icon css-1ebi949"><svg fill=
Remove 'link to' or similar - screen readers already announce it as a link
3.1.1 Språk på siden (1 avvik)
Testregel 3.1.1 (3.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Page is missing language declaration (×15 across article pages)

<html><head><meta charset="utf-8"/><meta content="width=device-width" name="viewport"/><title>Bereds
Add lang attribute to <html> element (e.g., lang='nb' for Norwegian Bokmål)
2.4.1 Hopp over blokker (1 avvik)

MODERATE
